In addition, several Shanghai Municipal Council officials are on-site to take care of and direct everything.

The Concessions' Interference in the Collection of Aviation Donations Arouses National Discontent; The Municipal Government Has Sent Personnel to Negotiate Separately; The Aviation Council Will Also Hold a Meeting to Respond

According to the Central News Agency, the interference by the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession and the patrol police of the French Concession in the collection of aviation salvation funds from the hotel industry, the confiscation of receipts, and the abuse of fines have been reported earlier. According to detailed information, the China Aviation Association received a letter from the Hotel Industry Association on the 12th of this month stating that at 2:00 PM on the 11th, the political department of the French Concession police summoned representatives of hotels such as the Asia, Da Hu, Da Fang, Guangtailai, Taian Inn, Ping An, Changjiang, and Taian Business Inn and obstructed the collection of aviation salvation funds in every possible way, imposing fines of 20 yuan on each establishment and threatening to increase the fine to 100 yuan if collections continued. The association asked the government to forcefully argue against this destruction of the patriotic movement. On the 19th, the association received another letter from the industry association, stating that in response to the unreasonable interference of the French Concession, an emergency meeting was convened to discuss countermeasures. While the meeting was in progress, successive reports were received from hotels in the Public Concession such as the Oriental, Great China, Jardine, Shenzhou, Central, New World, Great Jiangnan, Hongkou, and Lingnan, stating that personnel sent by the Municipal Council had ordered the surrender of all triplicate receipt books and account books for aviation salvation funds and forbade further collections, threatening to impose fines or revoke business licenses. Under this pressure, the businesses had no choice but to painfully suspend collections and requested that the association immediately forward a serious protest to the municipal government. The China Aviation Association, based on these letters, forwarded them for negotiation and replied to the industry association, stating that the authorities in the special district violated the will of the Chinese people by suppressing the aviation salvation movement and obstructing fundraising, which was unreasonable. The association said it had initiated separate negotiations and hoped that the industry association would promptly inform all members to continue their efforts to collect funds. Upon hearing the news, people from all walks of life paid close attention to the matter, because the collection of aviation salvation funds was entirely the result of the patriotic zeal of the Chinese people, who voluntarily and happily contributed. No one should interfere with this. The principle is obvious, but the concession authorities' unwarranted destruction of this effort goes against the principles of friendship. It is reported that the municipal government has sent secretaries Zhang Tingrong and Geng Jiaji to negotiate separately. The China Aviation Association will convene a board meeting in the coming days to discuss countermeasures.

Last Year's Imports of Annam Rice Amounted to 53 Million Yuan; Our Trade Surplus with France Was 15 Million; Our Trade Deficit with Annam Was 50 Million

According to the Shanghai Times News Agency, China's foreign trade has a large trade deficit every year. Last year, although Sino-French trade showed a surplus, there was a deficit with French Annam. If Annam's figures are included in those of France, China is in a trade deficit position. If we want to achieve a balance in international trade, the Chinese people must make efforts. The trade situation between the two countries last year is reported below.

Imports from France

China and France have had commercial relations for more than a hundred years. In the last few decades, with the exception of 1934, when China had a trade deficit, China has had a trade surplus in all other years. China's imports from France are mainly metals and mineral sands, but last year these items decreased compared to the previous year. A list of imports is extracted below: Metals, chemical products and pharmaceuticals, vehicles and boats, machinery and tools, wine, beer, spirits, drinking water, dyes, pigments, paints, varnishes, books, maps, paper skins, paper products, wool and its products, miscellaneous metal products, cotton, cotton yarn, candle soap, oils, fats, waxes, rosin, grains and grain flour, silk and rayon products, canned meats and vegetables, daily sundries, and others. Total imports last year amounted to 13,362,000 yuan.

Exports to France

China's exports to France are mainly textile fibers. Last year, exports of these products to France reached more than 14,194,000 yuan, a significant increase compared to the previous year, but less than in 1933. Animals and animal products totaled more than 3,631,000 yuan last year. Kernel sundries also increased last year, but tea exports declined, falling short of half of the previous year, and only a quarter compared to 1932. A list of China's important exports to France is listed below: Textile fibers, animals and animal products, kernels, wax, raw hides, tanned hides, leather goods, mineral sands, metals and metal products, piece goods, tea, plant-based dyes, and others. Total exports were 29,245,000 yuan. Compared between the two countries, China had a trade surplus of more than 15 million yuan.

Annam Rice Volume

Among China's trade relations with French colonies, Annam is the most important. From 1886 to last year, China had a large trade deficit. In 1932, the trade deficit was the largest, reaching 77,694,451 yuan. Although it decreased to 36,846,000 yuan in the previous year, it increased again to 57,000,003 yuan last year. The important reasons for this are: first, Annam obstructs and mistreats Chinese goods in many ways, and second, China's rice supply is insufficient, so it purchases large quantities of rice from Annam every year. Last year, Annam rice imports to China reached 53,850,226 yuan, an increase of 22,420,145 yuan compared to the previous year. This is also China's most serious problem. Although Annam grain imports decreased last year, they still amounted to 3,252,975 yuan. Coal also still amounted to 2,717,670 yuan. A list of Annam's important imports is listed below: Rice, grains, coal, cement, medicinal materials and spices, dried shrimp, sundries, salted fish, cotton, rubber, paint, leather goods, wood, dried fish, smoked fish, glue and rosin, and others. The total imports to China last year were 59,973,000 yuan.

Exports to Vietnam

China's exports to Annam are mainly silk, which also increased last year. Secondary items include metal ores, tea and paper products, including silk, metal ores, paper, miscellaneous textiles, vegetables, fruits, piece goods, charcoal coal, tea, tobacco, sundries, and others. The total value of goods exported from China to Annam last year was 5,644,000 yuan. After offsetting imports and exports, China's trade deficit reached more than 50 million yuan. Although China has a trade surplus with France, when combined with Annam, China still has a trade surplus of over 30 million. Those concerned about international trade must pay attention to this.

The Seamen's Party Headquarters Studies the Agenda of the International Labor Conference; The Seamen's Party Headquarters Special Commissioner's Office Orders Seamen's Organizations to Submit Reports by a Deadline

The China Aviation Society's Newly Manufactured Trainer Aircraft Scheduled for Test Flight on the 24th

According to the East China News Agency, in order to arouse the public's interest in aviation and to provide practice for its members, the China Aviation Society specially requested the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Office to trial manufacture a primary trainer aircraft, which began construction a month ago and has now been fully completed.

Domestic Materials

The aircraft is intended for training flights, so in addition to the pilot, it can seat one person. With the exception of the engine, which was purchased from the United States, all hardware, enamel, cedar wood, canvas, and all other small items are domestic products.

Form, Speed

According to Director Zeng Yijing of the Aircraft Office, who spoke to a reporter from the East China News Agency, the aircraft has 125 horsepower, a maximum speed of 115 miles per hour, a normal speed of 98 miles per hour, an altitude of 16,000 feet, a fuel capacity of 3 hours, and a weight of 1,600 pounds. It is a biplane amphibious type.

Scheduled Test Flight

The aircraft has now been completed and is being painted. It is scheduled to be test-flown at Longhua on the 24th of this month, and then Instructor Xu Chengqi will hand it over to the China Aviation Society for use by its members.

Shanghai's Foreign Trade for Two Months

According to the Shanghai Times News Agency, the Jianghai Customs released Shanghai's foreign trade figures for February yesterday, showing a sharp decrease in exports and an increase in imports, resulting in a trade deficit. January had a trade surplus of more than 1.3 million yuan, while February had a trade deficit of more than 17.7 million yuan. Therefore, Shanghai's trade deficit for two months was more than 16.3 million yuan. Among imported goods, metals and mineral sands still ranked first, and among exported goods, tung oil still ranked first. The Jianghai Customs investigated and reported on these matters as follows:

Current Trade Situation

In February of this year, the total value of Shanghai's foreign trade imports was 40,577,570 yuan (compared to 40,214,926 yuan in the same period last year), showing a clear increase compared to the import figure of 35,925,268 yuan in January. The total value of exports was 22,800,179 yuan (compared to 20,880,963 yuan in the same period last year), a sharp decrease of more than 14 million yuan compared to the export figure of 37,344,341 yuan in January. The trade deficit was 17,777,391 yuan. In the two months, the total value of Shanghai's imports was 76,529,838 yuan, a decrease compared to the same period last year. The total value of exports was 60,144,520 yuan, an increase compared to the same period last year. The trade deficit for two months was 16,385,318 yuan.

Imported Foreign Goods

In February, the main imported goods (in national currency units) were cotton at 3,887,764 yuan, wool and its products at 1,325,558 yuan, metals and mineral sands at 4,674,470 yuan, machinery and tools at 2,574,786 yuan, miscellaneous metal products at 2,463,518 yuan, chemicals at 2,135,560 yuan, pigments and dyes at 3,947,837 yuan, paper at 2,579,391 yuan, and wood at 1,258,404 yuan.

Exported Domestic Goods

In February, the main exported domestic goods were (in national currency units) pork at 709,061 yuan, eggs and egg products at 709,794 yuan, raw and tanned hides and leather goods at 2,220,648 yuan, tung oil at 5,481,630 yuan, sesame at 2,044,509 yuan, tea at 1,369,022 yuan, silk at 654,680 yuan, tungsten ore at 274,909 yuan, soybeans at 299,904 yuan, and rice husks at 156,953 yuan.

The Ministry of Industry Formulated Measures to Remedy Discrepancies in Measuring Instruments. Those with Larger Capacity Should Have the Mouth Shaved Down, and Those with Smaller Capacity Should Have the Wall Shaved Down.

According to National News Agency, after detailed research, the Ministry of Industry has formulated measures to remedy discrepancies in measuring instruments and has instructed the municipal government to comply with them. The measures are as follows: The proviso in Article 42 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Metrology Act is deleted. During the inspection of measuring instruments, if it is found that they exceed the prescribed tolerance, those with larger capacity should have the mouth shaved down or a wooden gauge nailed on, and those with smaller capacity should have the wall shaved down, and a separate seal should be affixed. If the measuring instruments of the buyer and seller are different in size but do not exceed the legal tolerance, they may be used interchangeably at the request of one party, and the other party may not refuse.

The Tobacco Industry in the French Concession Requests Exemption from Paying Business and Sanitation Fees

The Chinese Ratepayers Association of the French Concession received a report from the Second Branch of the Second District of the Citizens' Federation regarding the collection of fees from the tobacco industry by the Municipal Council and requested the Ratepayers Association to fight for justice. It has been learned that the original letter from the Ratepayers Association to the Municipal Council is as follows: According to a joint letter with the seals of ten tobacco shops, including Xinyutai, which specializes in selling Bing silk and does not sell other goods, the Municipal Council of the French Concession has been collecting tobacco fees on a monthly basis, and there are no other fees related to other types of tobacco. However, this year, the Municipal Council of the French Concession intends to collect classified business and sanitation fees from these shops, which is quite surprising. Upon investigation, the classified business and sanitation fee regulations only list the item "Tobacco Silk Warehouses" (with the note "Storage"). However, these shops are all retail stores and have no manufacturing facilities or storage areas. If the nature of the business is considered, these shops are actually the same as cigarette stores that sell cigarettes. Even larger cigarette stores also sell various types of Bing silk, such as raw silk, net silk, green leaf yellow tobacco, etc. Upon investigation, the aforementioned cigarette stores that also sell multiple types of tobacco do not have the name of classified business and sanitation fees. The situation of these shops is the same, but the scope is smaller, so there is no reason to pay classified business and sanitation fees. Therefore, we are submitting a statement of reasons, respectfully requesting you to forward it to the Municipal Council of the French Concession to achieve the purpose of canceling the aforementioned harsh taxes. We await your reply so that we can inform them.

The Qingpu-Shanghai Highway is Temporarily Open to Traffic. A Short-Term Contract Has Been Signed with China Motor Company to Operate. The Ticket Price is 1.20 Yuan Per Person.

Since the Qingpu-Shanghai Highway was completed, the public buses of the Qingpu-Shanghai Long-Distance Bus Company have not yet been completed. Therefore, a short-term contract has been signed with the China Motor Company on Malan Road to temporarily operate passenger cars between Shanghai and Qingpu. The ticket price is 1.20 yuan per person. A reporter from Central News Agency drove to inspect the entire route yesterday. The entire route starts from the Hongqiao Airport and goes directly to Zhongshan Park in Qingpu City, taking only 30 minutes. The entire road is relatively flat, but the road surface is too narrow, and it is very cramped for two cars to pass each other. There are a total of 22 bridges on the entire route, and 5 or 6 of them are quite high, which is too vertical, making driving on them slightly dangerous. The Qingpu-Shanghai Long-Distance Bus Company originally planned to hold a opening ceremony on April 1st and operate public buses with a ticket price of 80 cents per person. It is reported that the Shanghai terminus of the Qingpu-Shanghai Highway is adjacent to Hongqiao Airport, so it needs to be moved one kilometer south, and the relocation is currently being planned. It is feared that it will be difficult to open to traffic on schedule at that time.

Shanghai International Exhibition Seeks Participation from All Sectors

Site Located at the End of Yangshupu Road, Covering an Area of 200 Acres

Scheduled to Open Officially on July 1st

For the purpose of prospering the market and promoting international trade, Chinese and foreign people in this city have organized the Shanghai International Exhibition. The exhibition site is located on Yangshupu Road, covering an area of more than 200 acres. It is scheduled to open on July 1st. The preparatory office of the exhibition has sent letters to various factories and businesses seeking participation. Details are as follows:

Organizational Objectives

The organizational objective of the exhibition is to promote international trade. Shanghai has been a port for 95 years, and this is the first international exhibition. It is a good opportunity for Chinese national goods to attract foreign customers and expand sales. It is also possible to inspect the exquisite goods of other countries to serve as a model for improvement. The exhibition site is located on Yangshupu Road, on the banks of the Huangpu River, covering an area of more than 200 acres, about 2 million square feet, with convenient land and water transportation. All construction at the exhibition site is actively underway, and it is scheduled to open on July 1st and close in September.

Seeking Participation

The preparatory committee has been receiving a steady stream of letters and telegrams from merchants from various countries to discuss displays. At the same time, it is sending letters to various factories and businesses in this city seeking participation. Anyone with the following qualifications may participate in the exhibition: Manufacturers and producers from all over the world; import and export merchants or merchant factories or representatives of merchants or merchant organizations; various economic or travel organizations related to commerce; and various cultural institutions. Those who wish to participate can contact the preparatory committee of the Shanghai International Exhibition at No. 356 Jing'an Temple Road, Shanghai.

Opinions of Industry and Commerce

A reporter from New New News Agency met with Qian Chengxu of the General Chamber of Commerce of China yesterday and asked whether the Shanghai International Exhibition and the Shanghai Industrial Exhibition were the same organization. He replied that he had heard that the former was presided over by a Dutch merchant, and its location was at the old site of Shenxin No. 9 Factory on Yangshupu. Reading the English letterhead, it listed Guo Bingwen, Chen Guangfu, Du Yuesheng, Yu Zuoting, Lin Kanghou, and Miao Zhongxi as sponsors. The Chamber of Commerce received a brief invitation from the exhibition on the 20th of this month. At the same time, it investigated the sponsors listed on the letterhead and found that they were not fictitious. Therefore, it has attached its name as a sponsor. As for the organization of the Shanghai Industrial Exhibition, about two months ago, Mr. Millington, the manager of the Millington Advertising Company, a Shanghai foreign merchant, visited the Chamber of Commerce and showed a plan for displaying national goods to build Chinese-foreign commercial relations. After consideration, it was considered that the status of sponsor was not related to the organization itself, and its opening was in June next year. Therefore, he only allowed it to be a sponsor in the future. According to the company, the location is at the Shanghai Racecourse. In short, the Chamber of Commerce, in the position of a group, if its goal is proper and the participants are domestic celebrities, it can attach its name to it and assist it at any time to connect international emotions.

China Oil Lamp Company: Founding Plant Oil Lamps

Resisting Imported Kerosene; Economical and Safe; All Domestic Plant Oils Can Be Used

Mr. Zhong Ling, a native of Guangdong, has studied in France for many years and has a deep scientific background. Witnessing the difficulties of the times, he devoted his intelligence to research and experimentation, and finally invented the plant oil lamp that is popular throughout the country today. Its structure is completely based on scientific principles and refined, and all kinds of domestic plant oils can be used. The light is bright, even better than foreign lamps, and it saves oil, avoids fires, and has no toxic fumes. It can be said to have all the advantages of economy, safety, and hygiene. Its impact is to actively resist imported kerosene, prevent huge amounts of money from flowing out of the country, and on the passive side, to burn domestic oils and increase agricultural production. If a national war breaks out and the source of kerosene is cut off, domestic plant oils will be everywhere, so there is no need to worry about the lack of fuel. It has been approved and rewarded by the Ministry of Industry and has been granted a patent. His friends Chen Zuyi, Yao Shoukang, Ding Tingbiao, Zhong Hanli, Liao Fuya, Lu Jiyin, Xiao賀昌 et al., believe that the plant oil lamp invented by Zhong Ling is of great importance to the national economy and the people's livelihood, so they decided to prepare a company, open a factory to manufacture, and invited Chen Gongbo, Wei Huai, Lu Chao and other gentlemen to jointly launch the organization of the company, in order to proceed. Chen Zuyi was appointed as the director of preparation, and No. 218 Shandong Road, Shanghai, was selected as the location of the company. The capital amount was set at 150,000 national currency, and nearly half of it has been raised after a short period of recruitment. On the one hand, it has been submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for record, and has been approved, and on the other hand, a factory has been set up in Huade Road to manufacture. All management and transportation are carried out using scientific methods, in an orderly manner. The current products include wall lamps, table lamps, and glass lamps, which are of excellent quality and beautiful in style. (It is said that oil stoves and hanging lamps will be added in the future.) Under the rapid rotation of the spindle, thousands of lamps can be produced every day. At present, due to the high freight cost for transporting them to distant provinces, in order to reduce the consumption of customers, it is planned to set up branch factories in Guangdong, Sichuan, Jiangxi, and North China, which are currently under preparation. However, the North China branch factory has now been established and can deliver goods next month, with a daily output of 6,000 lamps. Wind and rain lamps will also be manufactured in the branch factory. Jiangxi Province has also recently organized a cooperative to promote the sale of Chinese oil lamps, and Chairman Xiong has sent staff to preside over the matter, which is also to promote domestic products. The governments of Sichuan and Guizhou provinces have also exempted local consumption taxes to encourage them, and central figures such as Chairman Lin, Wu Zhihui, and Huang Yingbai have either visited or requested lamps to test and burn them, and they have all praised them. At present, the manager's offices have been set up throughout the country, as well as in the Nanyang Islands, Annam, and India. The factory's shipments are almost in short supply. The company also believes that various vegetable oils in China already have their own sales channels on weekdays. Once the demand increases sharply, the price of oil will be affected. Therefore, it has submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry to issue a notice to the whole country to plant oil seedlings extensively, in order to increase oil production and keep oil prices low. It was approved by Circular No. 02055 and has been distributed to various provinces for planting. The company has also requested the National Economic Commission to issue a notice to silkworm farms to adopt oil lamps, in order to improve the results of silkworm rearing. It has also agreed to issue a notice.

Kidnapping Case in Datuan Town, Pudong; Bandits Punished

Zhang and Wang Each Sentenced to Twelve Years

Fang Guichang, a farmer in the countryside of Datuan Town, Fengxian County, Pudong, had a wealthy family and owned a lot of land, which attracted the attention of bandits. On November 12th of last year, they gathered a crowd, carried weapons, broke into the house, and looted clothes and silver dollars, worth more than one hundred yuan. Before leaving, they also kidnapped Fang Guichang's twelve-year-old grandson, Fang Degen, and hid him in the firewood room of Song Zhangsheng's house in Liujia Wuhu, Beisong Township, Fengxian County, to demand a ransom. Fang Guichang received many letters from the bandits, as many as eight, demanding a price of 24,000 yuan, which was finally reduced to 1,400 yuan. It was also stated that if there was no sincerity in contacting negotiations, they would decide to tear up the ticket. Fang Guichang was greatly frightened when he received the news, and reported to various police agencies, requesting investigation and rescue. Last month, the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau successively arrested six kidnappers in the case, including Yang Huangjin and Zhang Linfa, and rescued the hostage Fang Degen. They were handed over to the procuratorate of the local court for interrogation, and a public prosecution was filed. The other day, Judge Wu Xiangzu came to the court to publicly try the case and announced the verdict. Fang Hongsheng, Yang Huangjin, and Zhang Linfa were all sentenced to life imprisonment for jointly committing robbery and kidnapping for ransom, and were deprived of their civil rights for life. Zhang Kejin and Wang Genfu, two offenders, jointly committed robbery and kidnapping for ransom, and were sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment. Song Tangsheng was sentenced to six years of imprisonment for helping to intend to kidnap for ransom and kidnapping, and was returned to prison to await instructions after the judgment.

Gen Tai Factory Lawsuit Intricacies; Cheng Yize Has No Relationship

The Plaintiff's Application to Withdraw the Lawsuit Has Been Approved by the Court

Gen Tai Hehe Powder Factory, due to heavy debt, suddenly leased the factory to Hu Xiannan last year for operation. On the original brand name, the words "Yi Ji" were added. Later, the creditors of the factory, Siming Bank, learned that the factory owed more than 74,800 yuan in overdrafts, which had not been repaid for a long time. They leased the factory number privately, which was illegal. They filed a lawsuit against the factory owner Cheng Linsheng, Cheng's nephew Yize, manager Li Quanshen, and Hu Xiannan, claiming that they had changed their property and hindered their creditor's rights, and requested that the false lease contract signed by the defendants be declared invalid. The added word "Yi Ji" should be revoked, so that the original property of the first defendant would not be colluded and concealed, so that the plaintiff would not be in danger of creditor's rights. The First Special District Local Court had opened a court once. Cheng Linlin extended Tang Mingshi's lawyer's defense, saying that this lease did not hinder creditor's rights. Cheng Yize appointed Chen Zhen's lawyer, stating that he was not a shareholder of Gen Tai and was mistakenly implicated. The court then instructed to investigate and verify the case. Now, after the plaintiff, Siming Bank, investigated, it was determined that Gen Tai was indeed opened by Cheng Linsheng, and the lease was also done by Linsheng and his manager Li Quanshen. Cheng Yize was not a shareholder and had no relationship to the lease. He filed a statement stating the misunderstanding of suing Yize, and requested that the part of the lawsuit against Cheng Yize be withdrawn. After review by the trial judge, the decision was approved yesterday. As for the three defendants, Cheng Linsheng, Li Quanshen, and Hu Xiannan, they will still be summoned for trial at a later date.

China Anti-Tuberculosis Association Announces Tuberculosis Mortality Statistics for Various Countries

Over One Million Deaths, China Ranks First; Alarming Tuberculosis Mortality Rate in Five Major Cities

The number of deaths caused by tuberculosis in various countries around the world is very large, and China ranks first. In particular, the mortality rate in the five major cities is even more alarming. The report released by the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association is recorded as follows:

Tuberculosis Mortality Statistics for Various Countries

The number of people who died of tuberculosis in various countries around the world is: New Zealand 736, Canada 7,675, United Kingdom 41,103, United States 99,579, Netherlands 7,263, Germany 83,000, France 66,824, Italy 65,000, Japan 120,917, China 1,244,000, totaling 1,736,095. Other countries are not included because there are no statistics.

Number of Tuberculosis Deaths in Five Cities

The mortality rate of tuberculosis in China is mostly in cities, and less in rural areas. For example, the total number of deaths in Nanjing each year is 956, of which 179 died from tuberculosis. The total number of deaths in Shanghai is 1,748, of which 203 died from tuberculosis. The total number of deaths in Hankou is 1,427, of which 145 died from tuberculosis. The total number of deaths in Tianjin is 634, of which 73 died from tuberculosis. The total number of deaths in Hangzhou is 630, of which 23 died from tuberculosis. The number of tuberculosis deaths in the five cities accounts for more than 10% of the national total.

Villager Seeking Livelihood Encounters Swindler; Trusting Uncle Huang with Chicks, Attempting to Steal Chicks but Losing Money

Last winter, Xiaokui had come to Shanghai to seek a livelihood but failed. He took a train home. On the train, he met an old man with white hair, about sixty-two years old, and they chatted very harmoniously. Xiaokui told him about his efforts to seek a livelihood in Shanghai. The old man claimed to be surnamed Huang, so he was called Uncle Huang. He was working as an assistant accountant in a factory in Shanghai. Xiaokui then asked Uncle Huang to find him a job. When the train arrived at Suzhou's Guanqianli Station, the two got off the train together and went to Xiaokui's house for dinner. They stayed overnight, and the next morning, Uncle Huang left. Before leaving, he told Xiaokui that if there were vacancies for tea attendants in the factory after he returned to Shanghai, he would write to his family and invite them to Shanghai. Shen believed it to be true. The previous Saturday, he received a letter from Huang, signed Huang Shoucheng, saying that there was a foreman vacancy in his factory, with a monthly salary of twenty yuan, and an extra ten yuan or so. However, there were still chief accountants and managers in the factory, so a little bit of socializing fee of twenty to thirty yuan was needed. After receiving the letter, Xiaokui was overjoyed to have such a good job, so he borrowed thirty yuan in legal tender from relatives and friends, and brought a package to Shanghai yesterday, to meet at a certain tea house on Beijing Road. When he arrived, Uncle Huang was already there. When they met, they were extremely friendly. Xiaokui gave the socializing fee of thirty yuan in legal tender. Huang took him to a certain teahouse in the Buxianqiao area of the French Concession to wait. Not long after, a chief accountant, Mr. Zhang, arrived, talked a few words, and Zhang led Xiaokui to see the manager. Unexpectedly, Zhang suddenly disappeared halfway. Because Xiaokui was unfamiliar with the area, he couldn't find him for a while. When he returned to the tea house, Huang was also gone. He then realized he had been swindled. The package he was carrying, containing short shirts and pants, had been swindled away. Because he had no relatives or friends in Shanghai, he couldn't go home.

Weng Kelong Kidnapping Case: Dian Yaodong and Four Others Found to Be Involved

Weng Jingqing's fourteen-year-old son Kelong, the owner of Dehe Pawnshop in Chaozhou, located in Lanqi Wu Road, was kidnapped while on his way to Donghai School on Jingzhou Road at 7:00 AM on December 12th of last year. He was rescued. Subsequently, Chief Inspector Lu Liankui, Detective Liu Shaokui, Wang Chengying, and Detective Qian Xianting of the General Inspectorate arrested five criminals, Dong Xuezeng, Zhang Sheng, Dong Da, woman Zhu Han, and Dong Shi in the Shanghai Plantation Garden. They continued to arrest four accomplices, Tang Yaodong, Zhao Gouda, Xue 锦　, and Xue Chunrong, and sent them to the First Special Court separately. The details of the confession have been published in this newspaper. The trial judge Jiang Shuzi first sentenced Dong Xuezeng, Zhang Sheng, and Dong Da to nine years and six months in prison, and acquitted Zhu Han and Dong Zhu. The police needed to investigate Tang and the other four, and they were still detained. Yesterday, Judge Jiang continued the trial in the Third Criminal Court. Zhang Shizhu, the lawyer for the Public Works Department, stated that defendant Tang Yaodong admitted to having gone to the garden three times, Zhao Junda had been there once, and the handwriting in two of the ransom letters matched that of Xue 锦　 and Xue Chunrong. Then, witness Weng Peiyu testified that he had been ordered by his uncle Weng Jingqing to contact the bandits at the Xiaobai Ferry Bridge in Yangjing, Pudong, more than ten times, and had seen defendant Tang Yaodong on the scene twice. When questioned, the four defendants gave cunning answers. The court ordered them to be detained and rescheduled the verification.

Huang Jiefu, a shareholder of the Gongle Iron Factory on Linqing Road and a native of Jiangyin, received two threatening letters from bandits between the 7th and 8th of this month, with a bullet attached, demanding 30,000 yuan and instructing him to send someone to the Mayushan Road and Huade Road racecourse to negotiate the payment. A pistol and five bullets were found, and one bullet (the one attached to the letter) was sent to the First Court for interrogation and sentencing. Yesterday, 　　　judge　 court sentenced Li Zhongquan and Liu Xianshao to three years and six months in prison each, and the guns, bullets, and letters were confiscated.

They rummaged through boxes and cabinets and robbed a copper wire cable (worth more than one hundred yuan), four five-yuan banknotes, eight one-yuan banknotes, eight jiao in silver dollars, ten jiao in small silver coins, a black cotton padded jacket, a set of white flannel vests, and a pair of black serge trousers. Sichuan Guangyuan County Asks for Disaster Relief Due to Banditry

A telegram from the Sichuan Guangyuan County Charity Association reads: "Respectfully to all newspapers, we humbly submit that our Guangyuan is a mountainous area, historically known for its hardship. Since the founding of the Republic [of China], internal strife has been rampant. Our county is bordered by the provinces of Hubei, Shaanxi, and Gansu, and the constant movement of troops has exhausted the people with corvée labor. Later, warlords carved up the territory, extorting hundreds of thousands in military funds, compounded by corrupt local bullies who practiced layer upon layer of exploitation. The people had long been exhausted and at their wit's end, feeling as though there was no hope for survival. Unexpectedly, in the winter of the 21st year [of the Republic, i.e., 1932], the bandits of Sichuan invaded, Guangyuan was captured and recaptured three times over several years. The burning, killing, and plundering during this time were too numerous to describe. Fortunately, in the summer of the 24th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1935], our Central government's various divisions, together with the anti-bandit armies of this province, jointly suppressed the bandits, and the lost territories were gradually recovered. The people who had fled gradually returned. However, the autumn grain sowing season had already passed. Although they勉 try to plant, most of the crops were秀而不实. Autumn approaching, the government conscripted laborers to build fortifications and roads with utmost urgency. Before the work was completed, the food was already consumed. Now they have exhausted all edible葛根 tree roots and stripped all edible wild vegetables and fresh grass. The strong beg for food in all directions, while the weak die on the roads. The sight of abandoned children crying along the way is unbearable to hear. Moreover,抢食物之人 constantly emerge from villages and towns, surrendering themselves to the law, thinking there is糧食可食. The severity of the famine is imaginable. Fortunately, the military and political officials stationed in Guangyuan are promoting donations for relief, setting up shelters to care for children and hiring workers to bury corpses. However, the number of those seeking food and those dying of starvation is increasing daily, and it is impossible to sustain this with limited financial resources. The disaster-stricken people desperately need help. With our limited capabilities, we have repeatedly considered and can only beseech our military and political authorities and charitable philanthropists to show compassion and contribute generously. If you are willing to provide substantial funds for relief, please remit them to our county's Relief Sub-Association, so that hundreds of thousands of disaster victims can celebrate their revival. Your kindness would be akin to rebirth. We earnestly submit this plea and implore your attention. The Guangyuan County Charity Association, on behalf of hundreds of thousands of disaster victims, kowtows respectfully."

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: Shandong and the surrounding areas are sunny with strong northwesterly winds and sand. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River are hazy and warm, and still sunny with uncertain wind direction. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and this area have northwesterly to northeasterly winds. The East China Sea and Taiwan are cloudy with fog and northeasterly seasonal winds. The northern parts of Korea are snowing. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, the temperature in this city was 62.2 degrees as the highest, 37.0 degrees as the lowest. On the same day last year, the highest was 57.3 degrees and the lowest was 31.1 degrees.

From Zhaoguan to Huansha Creek

— Zhan Ruoye

Because of Wu Zixu's plea for troops, a well-known and significant place was created in history, and that is Zhaoguan. When Wu Yuan entered Wu through Jian Guan, he passed through Liyang (now He County), and begged for food from a silk-washing girl. The girl was ashamed, and threw herself into the creek to die. Later generations were touched by her chastity and martyrdom, and a shrine was built to worship her. This is the current Huansha Creek.

Zhaoguan is located outside the west gate of Hanshan County, twenty miles outside the city. The only means of transportation for this forty-mile round trip is a few donkeys. Zhaoguan is nestled among thousands of mountains, and the scenery is very majestic. The mountains overlap, with only this one pass, and there is nothing around it. Perhaps because the mountains are relatively high, Zhaoguan is contrasted as being so short and dark. Looking at it from a distance, it is even a little crooked! Seeing this, it is as if you are in a medieval ancient city, and a nostalgic feeling, no, an indescribable emotion, lingers in your heart. In this way, it can make you more convinced of the ancient saying that "a mud ball can seal Hangu Pass."

The Huansha Temple is in He County, but now it has become a nunnery. Its great name is not widely known to the locals, and its desolation is evident. When I went to explore this historical site with passionate emotions, I returned with a sense of disappointment. Readers, please don't use the fantasy of Ruoye Creek under Luoshan Mountain to read this Huansha Creek! It turns out that the so-called creek is just a pool of green water, without trees or mountains. The background is a row of earthen walls and several vegetable plots, that's all. And the impression it gave me was emptiness. Such a place has betrayed this beautiful place name with its rich poetic meaning.

Distributing Rice

— Qiao Yun Xun

The sages have two maxims: "For every grain of rice and every bowl of porridge, one should think of how hard it was to obtain!" In reality, among the large group of people who eat rice and porridge, how many can truly comprehend the meaning of these two sentences? It's no wonder, friends who are well-fed and clothed only know to "open their mouths when food comes" and "close their eyes when sleep comes." Who would think about maxims or anything else? Now there are two clear proofs that cannot be glossed over: in the crowded porridge distribution centers, one must "eat the whip first, then the porridge!" Every grain that enters the mouth is truly hard-earned. Without a desperate struggle and the efforts of the porridge distribution staff to maintain order, one cannot even hope to get half a spoonful of rice soup. "Eat the whip first, then the porridge!" is not just a descriptive phrase. There is also "Distributing Rice." Although this term is unfamiliar, anyone who has been a passenger on a river steamer once or twice will immediately recall the scene of "Distributing Rice." For example, on the Xiaochangjiang steamboats running the Shanghai-Yangzhou line, so-called steerage passengers pay less than one yuan in French currency for a journey of hundreds of miles, including the cost of meals. Although this is not exactly "charity," it can be considered a semi-charitable convenience provided to the common people by the company's management. Every time it comes to "Distributing Rice," a pair of bamboo chopsticks and a rough porcelain bowl are given. The bowl is neither Jingdezhen nor Yixing; perhaps it can be selected for an exposition in a thousand years! From afar, you can see the steaming yellow rice being carried out, basket by basket, by several junior boat crew members. This group of hungry tigers and eagles rush forward to grab it. It's more of a snatch than a distribution. This intense commotion is certainly greater than at the entrance of a porridge distribution center. Each person squats and swallows, while guarding against the small bundle under their buttocks being stolen. This tense atmosphere where hands, feet, ears, and eyes are all in use is a sight that eighteen painters could not capture. This coarse rice, naturally, even the dogs raised in wealthy families would not want to eat it, but for them, they can finish several bowls, as if eating delicacies. What do they eat with it? Four copper coins' worth of greens, or a bowl of vermicelli with fried tofu. At this time, the crying of children often creates a commotion. The women eat while humming lullabies, rocking their babies to sleep. What is called hell on earth? This is a miniature of it. They originally wanted to enter the metropolis to scrape together a living, but the metropolis is broken and withered, and they can't find a rice bowl. Before they even step onto the docks of the metropolis, they are given a preview. This scene of distributing and snatching rice probably symbolizes the difficulty of finding food in the metropolis.

Chapter 24: Love for Beauty Outweighs Duty; Worthy Men Cast Themselves into the Wilderness

Not only is the language that of that county, but the marriage customs are also maintained according to the customs of that county." We plan to leave tomorrow morning, I don't know if Mr. Cheng can make it in time!" Zhiqian did not expect to travel so quickly, and unconsciously took two breaths, showing a hesitant look, and reached out and touched his waist twice. World News

Japan's Death Penalty

— Ji Yun

In the past, Japan also practiced beheading and shooting, but now it mostly uses hanging. Generally, those who commit robbery and murder, arson and murder, or treason are likely to be sentenced to death. Very few people confess and are willing to serve their sentences after being sentenced to death in the first trial, and give up appealing. Most have to go through several appeals before being rejected and executed. In prison, death row inmates worry every time they hear the footsteps of the guards, asking if today is the day of execution. No matter what, the guards will not tell the death row inmates who cling to life the date of execution. They must take the death row inmate to the warden's office and read out "Today, according to the order of the Minister of Justice, the death penalty will be carried out" before the death row inmate knows that their death is imminent. At that time, handcuffs will be quickly added to prevent resistance. The evil prisoners who usually give up on themselves will change their expressions greatly at this time, their whole bodies trembling.

Next to the gallows, no one is willing to walk up on their own, and several people always have to carry them up by force. Crying, screaming, raging, calling for injustice, it can be said to be the most tragic moment in life. Only female prisoners rarely riot, except for crying. Next to the gallows is a Buddhist altar set up for the death row inmate to pray. In front of the Buddha are a few steamed buns and a cup of tea, provided for the death row inmate to eat before death. Some people eat these steamed buns, but their hands are already trembling so badly. The cup of tea is always spilled.

Former Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce Councilor Yuta Ken was known for his composure at the time of execution. Because his rice business failed, he borrowed money from usurers, and could not repay it. He incited two students to beat the usurer to death with baseball bats, cut him into several pieces, put him in wooden boxes, and threw him into the water. Later, the matter was leaked, and this agricultural scholar and high-ranking official of the Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce became a prisoner. When he was executed, he was calm, ate two steamed buns, drank a cup of tea, thanked the guards and the executioners, and then calmly stepped onto the stage. His sister knew the date of execution and sent a white vest, covered with the words "Namu Amida Butsu." She thought that wearing it during the execution could reduce suffering.

Except for political prisoners and special offenders, death row inmates all live in the same room, because they are afraid of suicide. Only the prisoner named Damai Longyun was imprisoned alone because he was so vicious that he robbed other people's food. He was a big thief who committed adultery, theft, murder, and arson. It is not known how many nuns in various parts of Japan were humiliated by him. Living in prison, he could not get enough to eat, so he forced the guards to buy bread and snacks. He had no money. The guards had no choice but to get his consent to sell his dead body in advance to a certain university as an anatomy specimen, earning 30 yen. Selling his future dead body to feed himself lavishly, I'm afraid Damai Longyun of Japan must be the first person to do so.

Little Spring and Autumn Weekly

Zhanzhan Records

— (Zhang Ge)

Mr. Cai Yuanpei once said: "Modern youth should have three basic conditions: the physical strength of a lion, the agility of a monkey, and the spirit of a camel." Everyone knows that this is a very valuable statement. Mr. Huang Renzhi's three conditions for the Chinese people also have the same value. He said: "China must have the spirit of Russia, the science of Germany, and the wealth of the United States. If these three things are combined, China will become strong without even trying."

There were two foreigners named Ma in history. One compared China to paradise, while the other compared China to hell. The former is Marco Polo's "Travels of Marco Polo," and the latter is Malthus's "Essay on the Principle of Population." Some people think that these two people's views are too extreme. In fact, if we observe society carefully, we can see that one side is paradise and the other side is hell.

Imperial Kitchen Tofu

— Zhe Cun

Song Muzhong's "Xipi Leigao" records the southern tour of the Qing Emperor Shengzu and commemorates the grand occasion of welcoming him during the tenure of the Jiangsu Governor. One day, a court eunuch bestowed food, saying that Song Luo was an old minister, different from other governors, and should be bestowed in the same manner as generals and governors. It also conveyed an imperial edict saying: "I have a daily tofu dish, the taste is unusual. Since Governor Song is an elderly man, let the imperial kitchen eunuch teach it to the governor's cook, so that he can enjoy it for the rest of his life." Liang Zhilin, Vice Minister of Fujian, once included it in his "Random Notes on Strange Tales," but regretted that the method was not passed on to outsiders. Later, he accidentally read "Suiyuan Shidan," which contained eight-treasure tofu, also a recipe given by the Qing Emperor Shengzu to Xu Jian'an, Minister of the Ministry of Rites. When the Minister obtained the recipe, the imperial kitchen spent one thousand taels of silver. The method is to cut tender tofu into small pieces, add fragrant mushroom powder, hemp mushroom powder, pine nut kernels, melon seed kernels, almond kernels, etc., and other ingredients such as shredded chicken, shredded ham, and diced bamboo shoots, stir-fry in thick chicken broth, and serve. Use a ladle instead of chopsticks to eat it. It is especially suitable for eating. This should be no different from the tofu given to Song Muzhong. I believe that with such a combination of cooking, any food should be delicious and palatable, not just tofu. It can also be seen that in the past, autocratic emperors indulged in extravagance with jade food in all directions.

Inverse Law

— Xiao Jun

Recently, I discovered a law: the younger the person, the bigger the ego; the older the person, the smaller the ego. If you don't believe me, listen to me:

The staff in the agency, such as junior clerks and assistant staff, all wear shiny badges of the XX Department XX Hall, hanging on their collars, looking very proud. As for the XX Director and XX Chief, they don't wear badges.

Students in provincial schools who have poor academic performance, bad character, and are in lower grades, or even students in cram schools, wear badges all day long. As for students who have good academic performance, good character, and are in higher grades, they don't wear badges.

Even people in society who have no knowledge and no cultivation talk eloquently and make ghosts and gods pale. As for people who have knowledge and cultivation, they never talk much.

One Head Sleep and Two Head Sleep

— Qian Meizhang

Husband and wife are clearly sleeping head-to-head, but it is called "one head sleep." On the contrary, sleeping head-to-toe is called "two head sleep." The logic is incomprehensible. I would like to ask dialectologists about this.

European Customs Wedding Gifts

— Ji Yijie

According to European customs, when relatives and friends get married, they must continuously give wedding gifts up to sixteen times. Moreover, the time and materials are fixed, unlike our country, where gifts are only given at the time of marriage, and the quantity and quality of the gifts are all up to the giver. Now, I will record the time and materials of the European wedding gifts for readers.

The first year is called the "Paper Wedding," and gifts made of paper are given. The second year is called the "Grass Wedding," and gifts made of grass are given. The third year is called the "Sugar Wedding." The fourth year is called the "Leather Wedding." The fifth year is called the "Wood Wedding." The seventh year is called the "Flower Wedding." The tenth year is called the "Tin Wedding." The twelfth year is called the "Linen Wedding." The fifteenth year is called the "Crystal Wedding." The twentieth year is called the "Porcelain Wedding." The twenty-fifth year is called the "Silver Wedding." The thirtieth year is called the "Pearl Wedding." The thirty-fifth year is called the "Coral Wedding." The fortieth year is called the "Jade Wedding." The fiftieth year is called the "Gold Wedding." The seventy-fifth year is called the "Diamond Wedding." Based on the names of the paper, grass, sugar, leather, and wood weddings, gifts are made with their materials. The intention is nothing more than to take the meaning that the longer the marriage lasts, the stronger the love becomes. To use this as a blessing has a profound meaning. May those who become husband and wife in the morning and sigh at parting in the evening take note.

The Human World

The late American humorist Mark Twain said: "A person who is pessimistic before the age of forty-eight knows too much; a person who is optimistic after the age of forty-eight knows too little." This sentence is not "humorous," but rather has a very strong sense of sadness.

Is it really "most pitiable is the human world"? (Zi Ying)

Four-Mile Flatland Cross-Country Race: Uneven Grouping Leads to Chinese Runners Being Eliminated; All Three Spots Taken by Russians; Key Athletes Like Wang Zhengling Absent, Greatly Reducing Strength

The four-mile open flatland cross-country race, organized by the Westerners' Athletic Association, was held at Hongkou Park yesterday morning at 10:30 AM. The race rules stipulated that the starting order would be determined based on the usual performance standards of each racer. Initially, there were 43 participants, but ten key athletes, including Wang Zhengling, Wu Wenlin, Ling Xuewen, Zhang Liang, Xu Yanbo, Pan Gongbao, and Lifu Qinggu, were absent at the last minute. As the time arrived, 43 athletes gathered in front of the dressing room inside the west gate of Hongkou Park. The starter, Mike Na, blew the whistle, and the two weakest competitors, He Dequi and Xia Honggeng, started first. Subsequently, a group was released every 30 seconds until 10:30:30 AM, when the last group was released.

This race's grouping was exceptionally balanced, which should have led to fierce competition. Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (Part Two) (Zero) (Eight)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

At that moment, Mr. March came over and stopped, saying a few words of comfort and encouragement, "My dear, you have already done your best to promote that good state. Continue to maintain your faith, your efforts, and the success of your small experiment will prove it is not in vain." This good man never lost his belief in humanity, still hoping to see peace, goodwill, and happiness fill the earth.

"Father, I don't have such extravagant hopes. I only wish to give these children a home where they can learn some simple qualities, so that when they enter the vast world to make their own way, their hardships may be reduced somewhat. Honesty, courage, diligence, faith in heaven, in people, and in themselves; that is what I strive for here."

"That is everything. Give them these aids, and then let them lead independent and honorable lives; no matter what success or setbacks they encounter, I think they will always remember and bless your efforts, my good son-in-law and good daughter."

At this time, the professor had already joined their group; as Mr. March spoke, he extended both hands, one to his son-in-law and one to his daughter, and when he looked at them, they felt immense comfort. Later, Shu and her husband stood side by side for a while, talking quietly, feeling that their "summer cultivation," having received the approval of that wise elder, must be very good.

Economic Publication

The Trend of Soviet Economic Policy

— Wei Yuan

Soviet economic policy has gone through several different methods. Generally speaking, it can be divided into four periods: First, from 1917 to 1921, the period of military communism; second, from 1921 to 1928, the period of the New Economic Policy; third, the first Five-Year Plan period; and fourth, the current second Five-Year Plan period.

During the first period, the Soviet government attempted to control the complete economic life of the country. Although this could not be fully implemented at all times and in all places, it was indeed an important motivation in the Soviet government's rule during this period.

The second period, the New Economic Policy period, differed from the first period in that it abandoned the principle of state economic control and monopoly that was practiced in the first period. The New Economic Policy was a dual system. On the one hand, the government retained control over almost all heavy industries, virtually the entire credit system, international trade, and transportation. On the other hand, it allowed farmers to cultivate their own land and trade freely.

During the third period, the government monopolized various products and trade, paying close attention to agriculture. The individual peasant system based on individuals was abolished and replaced by a collective system. The sale of agricultural products in the market was prohibited. Prices were fixed and unchangeable. Consumption was strictly limited. The government took control of the nation's production and distribution, and the authorities obtained huge amounts of grains and other agricultural products at fixed prices. From this point of view, the authorities were successful. However, the authorities were not successful in increasing or improving agricultural products, because private property was not allowed in collective farms, and farmers had to sell the surplus at low fixed prices. Another point is that the authorities could not eliminate the illegal free markets, because the prices in the free markets were several times higher than those set by the government.

The characteristic of the fourth period is that the government granted privileges to farmers. Once farmers delivered the portion stipulated in the Five-Year Plan to the government, the government allowed them to sell the remaining goods at high prices in the free market. In this way, it could somewhat compensate them for the losses they suffered from selling at fixed prices. Since January 1933, when collective farms were specially allowed to trade, the free market, except for a few restrictions, became legal again. From then on, in addition to state grain agencies distributing products to workers and employees at low fixed prices, the state and cooperative stores also had parallel development with trade far exceeding the unified system prices. Therefore, the price system naturally became increasingly chaotic. The Soviet ruble was not a standard of uniform value, and its purchasing power varied from place to place depending on local conditions. The level of nominal wages could no longer induce workers to increase production. Moreover, the government, based on past experience, had realized that universal distribution control was not only very uneconomical but also very difficult to handle. The government also understood that controlling supply was detrimental to agricultural development and the improvement of goods consumed the most. For the above reasons, the Soviet government abolished fixed price control supply and the fixed grain card system in January 1935, and created a uniform price level for each commodity.

During the first Five-Year Plan period, there was also a basic principle—that is, the "complete" collectivization of agriculture. The Soviet government also needed to reconsider this. Later, several private farms were allowed in the collective system. The new law in February 1935 stipulated that "the fruit plots used by collective farms, excluding the land occupied by houses, may occupy one-quarter to one-half of a hectare, and those in abnormal areas may occupy one hectare": "Each collective farm in the planting areas of grains, cotton, sugar beets, flax, hemp, potatoes, and vegetables may raise for its own use: one cow, two calves, one sow, and its young animals—if the management of the collective farm considers one sow insufficient, it may raise two sows and its young animals—no more than ten sheep and goats, an unlimited number of hens and rabbits, and no more than twenty beehives." In agricultural areas with livestock breeding, each collective farm may raise for its own use: two or three cows and two or three or more heads of livestock; in nomadic areas, the collective farm may raise for its own use: eight to ten cows, a total of one hundred to one hundred and fifty sheep and goats, an unlimited number of hens, no more than ten horses, and five to six camels. In this way, the existence of private farms in the collective system has been recognized as legal, and the private interests of the centralized farms are also encouraged. As a result, a considerable increase in the general agricultural products has been achieved.

Another feature of this period is that the Soviet government does not legally stipulate the maximum production volume. This method was adopted during the first Five-Year Plan. Although the completion of each department of the Five-Year Plan was different, the planned estimates increased year after year. As a result, due to the skills of workers and technicians, trying to force excessive production inevitably had a negative impact on production standards. This mistake was recognized by the Soviet authorities. Now attention is paid to improving the quality of products, and the requirement for quantity is reduced to moderate. If this statement is correct, then the quantity required in the 1935 plan should be less than that of 1934. In the 1935 plan, the 1935 plan has taken into account the strength of domestic industry, and not focused solely on increasing output. In this way, the completion of each department of this plan is more balanced. Now, there is progress in both the quality of industrial and agricultural products, and the authorities' attitude towards manual and technical personnel has also changed. The new regulations stipulate that there is a significant difference in the wage standards between skilled and unskilled workers.

These new trends are very obvious in the Soviet domestic economic policy and various state-owned enterprises—the reorganization of ordinary schools and universities, the revision of the constitution to democratize the election system, the estimation of remuneration for manual and mental work, and the combination of state-owned and private industries.

Under the current economic system, except for private farms inside and outside collective farms, all are run by state-owned or state-managed agencies, while under the New Economic Policy system, only economic enterprises related to the military are directly managed by the state.

This change in Soviet economic policy is a very important matter. The Soviet Union is trying to promote private enterprises on the one hand and implement state economic control on the other. It is impossible to predict now how far it will develop in the future, but the attempt itself is undoubtedly true and far-sighted.

The Trend of Soviet Industry Under the Stakhanovite Movement

— He Bing

(I)

Regarding the Soviet Stakhanovite movement, there have been several introductions in the country, but few have mentioned the actual effects this movement has already had in the Soviet Union. This movement can be said to be the most important feature of the Soviet Union's second Five-Year Plan, and it is also a further manifestation of the Soviet Union's socialist economic construction. This movement has not only ignited the enthusiasm of young men and women across the Soviet Union, but even advanced capitalist countries are astonished by the fact that production efficiency has been raised to the highest possible technical standards at the time.

What is the Stakhanovite movement? It is the improvement of industrial efficiency. Stakhanov was originally an ordinary coal miner in the "Central Irmino Coal Mine" of the Soviet Union's "Simply Speaking Donbas Mining Area," but suddenly became world-renowned, known as the "Hero of Labor" and a "Heroic Figure in History." Starting from November 14th last year, Moscow held a grand Stakhanovite Movement Congress. According to the report of Stakhanov himself, the originator of the Stakhanovite movement, the movement occurred because the work efficiency in the coal mine where he worked was extremely slow. He and his comrades had long wanted to find a way to improve it. Finally, on September 1st last year, he mined 102 tons of coal in six hours, and on September 9th, it increased to 175 tons, filling eleven freight cars, creating a world record. The average mining volume of each worker in this mining area was originally only six to seven tons, while Stakhanov alone exceeded the labor efficiency of "twenty-five people."

Now, the Soviet Union's rulers have promoted the Stakhanovite movement to all departments, and even popularized it in the fields of military affairs and culture. The Stakhanovite movement has become a lever for promoting the Soviet Union's entire socialist construction. Originally, the Soviet Union had long launched movements to improve production technology and increase labor productivity. In 1919, Lenin said, "In the final sense, the most important issue is the efficiency of labor production, which enables the new social institutions to win. Capitalism has created labor production efficiency never seen in the era of slavery. Similarly, because socialism creates newer and higher labor production efficiency, it can thoroughly overcome capitalism." During the first Five-Year Plan era, the Soviet Union put forward the slogans "Strive for new technology" and "Technology is enough to solve everything." In order to transform from an agricultural country to an industrial country, a large-scale "shock brigade" movement was launched, attracting countless industrial workers to become shock brigade members, fully instilling them with technical knowledge. If the shock brigade movement is regarded as the representative feature of the first Five-Year Plan, then the Stakhanovite movement is the representative feature of the second Five-Year Plan. In terms of its effectiveness and influence, it is naturally a further step than the shock brigade movement. However, Stakhanov's success is based on past construction. As Stalin said, during the shock brigade movement, workers often lacked technical knowledge, so it was very difficult, but now, although there is still a gap between physical labor and mental labor, young workers with technical knowledge have become very popular.

The occurrence of all movements has actual needs, that is for sure. The reason why the Stakhanovite movement can succeed in the Soviet Union, leaving aside other conditions, is that the Soviet Union's current industry—especially heavy industry—has a great need for technical improvement. Conversely, even in industrialized countries such as Britain and the United States, at a time of overproduction, the original technology is still declining. Not only will new technologies not occur, but the need for them is also very small.

Originally, although the Soviet Union's industry has made rapid progress since the revolution, because it was originally a backward agricultural country, some industrial sectors still could not develop as planned. During the second Five-Year Plan, what the Soviet authorities found most difficult was that several major heavy industrial sectors were quite sluggish. If the problems could not be overcome, the Soviet Union's crisis would be extremely serious.

1935 was the third year of the Soviet Union's second Five-Year Plan. Although various heavy industries continued to progress over the years, the distance from the original plan was still very large. Taking ironmaking, coal mining, and oil as examples, the planned ironmaking target for the ironmaking industry in 1935 was:

Pig iron: 12.5 million kilograms

Steel: 12 million kilograms

Rolled steel: 8.5 million kilograms

But by the end of June last year, the production of pig iron was 6.04 million kilograms, only reaching 48% of the plan, and was even less than the 10 million kilograms achieved in 1934. The steel production volume was less than 6 million kilograms in the same period, which was even less than that of pig iron. The same is true for rolled steel, which did not achieve the intended purpose.

The planned coal mining target for 1935 was 102.2 million kilograms. In the first half of last year, the production volume was 49.78 million kilograms, equivalent to 45.5% of the plan for that year. The plan for May, July, August, and September and later was also not completed. The sluggishness of the coal mining industry in the Soviet Union's heavy industry is very obvious. In August last year, the Soviet government issued a warning: "The shortage of fuel in the Soviet Union has a great impact on the national economy. The sluggishness of the coal mining industry should be resolved immediately."

The Soviet Union has spent a lot of effort on the organization and technology of the oil industry, so it has been making progress day by day in recent years. In 1934, the Soviet Union's oil industry had already ranked second in the world, only behind the United States, but according to the Soviet Union's planned plan and domestic situation, the distance is still far. In 1934, oil production reached 88.8% of the planned plan. In terms of its storage capacity, the quantity is actually too small (the Soviet Union's total oil resource storage accounts for 32% of the world's total, more than 30 billion kilograms). In 1935, it was planned to extract 33.33 million kilograms of oil (including oil and gas), but it was not actually achieved. Even the Soviet Union's famous "Grozny" oil field has reduced its production volume.

In such a situation, how to develop these heavy industries is naturally what the Soviet authorities are worried about. Upon seeing Stakhanov's success, they will inevitably use it as a grand movement to promote it in various industrial sectors.

(II)

What impact has the Stakhanovite movement had on the Soviet Union's various industrial sectors? Generally speaking, as of today, several sectors have already increased their production volume by three to five times compared to before. In particular, in the coal mining industry, where the Stakhanovite movement originated, the results are even more remarkable. The Voroshilov Coalfield and the Sverdlovsk Coalfield have performed particularly well, and completely completed the previous year's plan by the end of November last year. That is, the Voroshilov Coalfield reached 104.7% of the estimated production volume at the end of November, and the Sverdlovsk Coalfield also reached 100.2%. In other industrial sectors, world records for production efficiency have also continued to occur. According to the calculations of the Soviet Union's famous technician Kurasov-Sese, since the start of the Stakhanovite movement, the labor production efficiency of heavy industry has generally increased by 16.3%. This number is very surprising.

Now, let's briefly describe the technical improvements in the various heavy industrial sectors under the influence of the Stakhanovite movement.

(1) Ironmaking industry: As mentioned above, the Soviet Union's ironmaking industry was originally sluggish, but since the Stakhanovite movement occurred, by December last year, the Soviet Union's daily production volume had:

Steel: 40,000 kilograms

Pig iron: 38,500 kilograms

Regulations, steel exceeded pig iron. The technical improvement of the ironmaking sector is even more vigorously carried out. According to Soviet newspapers:

(2) Coal mining industry: The coal mining industry was very sluggish in the first half of last year, but it recovered from the second half of the year. At the end of November last year, the Soviet Union's national production performance reached 93.5% of the planned target, and there were very few that did not reach it. And in the Stakhanovite birthplace, the Ruhr Coalfield, the results are even more amazing. Each coal mining machine can mine an average of 17 tons, while the highest in the United Kingdom is only 11 tons. The average output of coal per shift is 60 tons, breaking the highest record in the United States.

(3) Oil industry: Although the Soviet Union's oil industry has made significant progress, there are still many shortcomings. The completion of the planned plan is greatly hindered by this. The Soviet Union's drilling technology level is lower than that of the United States. This drilling plan will be the basic prerequisite for expanding production in the future. However, this is only in general terms. In the Stakhanovite-style oil extraction sector, its outstanding performance is another matter. Especially in Moinerf Chech, engineer Nitchi Qing's drilling speed broke the American record. For those who have suffered from leukorrhea for a long time due to physical weakness, taking "Car-Schaudinn" and "Corpol" at the same time can often cure the disease in a short period of time. After recovery, they can have children as usual. This treatment can be done at home. I heard that many women have recently adopted this self-treatment method and have been cured.

Dr. Yao Juyan's Clinical Report on Gonorrhea

Clinic: Corner of Sichuan Road and Ningbo Road Hours: 10 AM to 6 PM

Reasons for Difficulty in Curing Chronic Leucorrhea and Methods for Thorough Treatment

Everyone knows that chronic leucorrhea is difficult to cure. Based on my years of clinical experience, if someone who has suffered from gonorrhea has sexual intercourse with a woman even once, there is a possibility of infecting the other person; the female vaginal tract is a suitable place for gonococci to survive. Therefore, even if an unclean man has only one sexual encounter with a woman, and the man's gonorrhea has been proven to be eradicated by a doctor, if he later has sexual intercourse with the woman, the gonococci from the woman will still infect the already cured man. If this mutual infection continues, how can gonorrhea ever be eradicated?

When I encounter gonorrhea patients with wives, whether it is new or old gonorrhea, I use two treatment methods: first, I treat the man's old gonorrhea with anti-gonorrhea serum and electric therapy, and at the same time administer the internal medicine "Clinnon." On the other hand, I instruct the patient's wife to take "Clinnon" internally and use German "Car-Schaudinn Vaginal Tablets" to insert into the vaginal tract. If there are gonococci in the vaginal tract, they will all die when they encounter this medicine. Since I have used this treatment method, the results have been exceptionally good. Even if it is chronic leucorrhea for many years, it will never recur after it is cured. For those with wives who have gonorrhea, regardless of whether they have infected their wives, it is always best for their wives to use "Car-Schaudinn Vaginal Tablets," so that those with gonorrhea can treat gonorrhea, and those without gonorrhea can also ensure that they are not infected by gonorrhea. This is indeed a one-shot, two-bird approach.
